 privansion of karpshan act kii dhara 13 (1) (D) ke tahat apane yaa kisi duusare ke phaayde ke liye pad kaa durupyog karne or dhara 13 (2) ke tahat lok sevak ke pad par rahete hue criminal missconduct ke liye ek se saat varsh tak kii sajaa kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 Also, a provision has been made to impose a fine on such convicts
 iske alaava bhartiya dand samhita yani ipisi kii dhara 420 ke tahat chal karne or beimaani se sampatti dene ke liye uksaane ko aparaadh banaaya gaya he, jiske liye saat varsh kii sajaa or jurmaane kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he

 About 50 vehicles were found which were parked in the parking lot for a long time of 5-7 years
 arpeef ke diji arun kumaar ne bataaya ki desh bhar ke 326 steshnon par 9 se 11 agast ke bich ye abhiyaan chalaaya gaya
 There was a doubt about whether these vehicles were left in the parking lot in any crime
 In this regard, police of different states have also been written for investigation by giving details of these vehicles
 aankade bataate hai ki 50 gaadiyaan 5-7 saal ke lambey vakt se padi thim jabaki 3000 gaadiyaan 5 dinon se zyaada vaqt se
 This was investigated before Independence Day
 dilli or uske aasapaas ke stesan parking main 128 gaadiyaan 5 dinon se bhi zyaada vaqt se khadi milin
 And if three vehicles were found stolen, an FIR was lodged
 jabaki sandehaaspad gadiyon kii jaanch chal rahi he
